Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Luminary 131 (Apollo 13) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 001 OF AGC PROGRAM LMY99 BY NASA 2021112-061
	16:27 JULY 14,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

021217,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     Part of the source code for Luminary 1A build 099.

021235,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              and corrected the errors found.

021260,000047:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021261,000048: 
021262,000049:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021263,000050: 
021264,000051:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021265,000052:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021266,000053: 
021267,000054:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021268,000055: 
021269,000056:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021270,000057:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021271,000058:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021272,000059:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021273,000060: 
021274,000061:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021275,000062: 
021276,000063:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021277,000064: 
021278,000065:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021279,000066: 
021280,000067:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021281,000068:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021282,000069:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021283,000070:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021284,000071:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021285,000072:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021286,000073:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021287,000074:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021288,000075:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021289,000076:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021290,000077: 
021291,000078:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021292,000079: 
021293,000080:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021294,000081:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021295,000082: 
021296,000083:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021297,000084: 
021298,000085:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021299,000086: 
021300,000087:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021301,000088: 
021302,000089:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021303,000090: 
021304,000091:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021305,000092: 
021306,000093:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021307,000094: 
021308,000095:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
021309,000096: 
021310,000097:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021311,000098: 
021312,000099:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
021313,000100: 
021314,000101: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021315,000102: 
021316,000103: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021317,000104: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021318,000105: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021319,000106: 
021320,000107: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021321,000108: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
021322,000109: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
021323,000110: 24,2000           05327        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
021324,000111: 24,2001           00004                           OCT      4

021729,000516:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021730,000517: 
021731,000518:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021732,000519:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021733,000520:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021734,000521: 
021735,000522:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021736,000523: 
021737,000524:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021738,000525:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021739,000526:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021740,000527:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021741,000528: 
021742,000529:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021743,000530: 
021744,000531:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021745,000532: 
021746,000533:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021747,000534: 
021748,000535:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL                                        FLAGUP
021749,000536:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      ENDOFJOB
021750,000537:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)                     WAITLIST
021751,000538:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER                                        FINDVAC
021752,000539: 
021753,000540:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021754,000541: 
021755,000542:                                                                                                  #        P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021756,000543:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021757,000544: 
021758,000545:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021759,000546: 
021760,000547:                                                                                                  #        NONE
021761,000548: 
021762,000549:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021763,000550: 
021764,000551:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021765,000552: 
021766,000553:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021767,000554: 
021768,000555:                                                                                                  #        TRACKFLG, P25FLAG
021769,000556: 
021770,000557:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021771,000558:

021827,000614:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)

021843,000630:                                                                                                  #        UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME

022033,000820:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
022034,000821:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022035,000822: 
022036,000823:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022037,000824:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022038,000825: 
022039,000826:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022040,000827: 
022041,000828:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
022042,000829:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
022043,000830: 
022044,000831:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022045,000832: 
022046,000833:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
022047,000834:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
022048,000835: 
022049,000836:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022050,000837: 
022051,000838:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
022052,000839:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
022053,000840:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
022054,000841:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
022055,000842: 
022056,000843:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
022057,000844:                                                                                                  #        
022058,000845:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
022059,000846:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
022060,000847: 
022061,000848:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022062,000849: 
022063,000850:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
022064,000851:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
022065,000852:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
022066,000853: 
022067,000854:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022068,000855: 
022069,000856:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
022070,000857: 
022071,000858:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022072,000859: 
022073,000860:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
022074,000861: 
022075,000862:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022076,000863: 
022077,000864:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
022078,000865: 
022079,000866:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

022258,001045:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022259,001046:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022260,001047: 
022261,001048:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022262,001049:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022263,001050: 
022264,001051:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022265,001052: 
022266,001053:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022267,001054: 
022268,001055:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022269,001056: 
022270,001057:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022271,001058: 
022272,001059:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022273,001060: 
022274,001061:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022275,001062:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022276,001063: 
022277,001064:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022278,001065: 
022279,001066:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022280,001067:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022281,001068:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 +P20
022282,001069: 
022283,001070:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022284,001071: 
022285,001072:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022286,001073: 
022287,001074:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022288,001075: 
022289,001076:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022290,001077: 
022291,001078:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
022292,001079: 
022293,001080:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
022294,001081: 
022295,001082: 24,3135     1143                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
022296,001083: 24,3135                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
022297,001084: 24,3135           05504        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
022298,001085: 24,3136           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
022299,001086: 24,3137           00004                           INHINT                                         
022300,001087: 24,3140           04674                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
022301,001088: 24,3141           40140                           CADR     SETMINDB                              
022302,001089: 24,3142           00003                           RELINT                                         
022303,001090: 24,3143           34736        R23LEM1            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ENABLE TRACKER
022304,001091: 24,3144           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022305,001092: 24,3145           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                
022306,001093: 24,3146           33205                           CAF      OCT205                                
022307,001094: 24,3147           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022308,001095: 24,3150           20623                           CADR     GOPERF1

022310,001097: 24,3152           03154                           TC       R23LEM11                              #  PROCEDE

022342,001129:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022343,001130:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022344,001131: 
022345,001132:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022346,001133:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022347,001134: 
022348,001135:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022349,001136: 
022350,001137:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022351,001138:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022352,001139:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022353,001140: 
022354,001141:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022355,001142: 
022356,001143:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022357,001144:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022358,001145:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022359,001146:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022360,001147: 
022361,001148:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022362,001149: 
022363,001150:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022364,001151:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022365,001152:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022366,001153: 
022367,001154:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022368,001155: 
022369,001156:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022370,001157:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022371,001158:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022372,001159: 
022373,001160:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022374,001161: 
022375,001162:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022376,001163: 
022377,001164:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022378,001165: 
022379,001166:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022380,001167: 
022381,001168:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022382,001169: 
022383,001170:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022384,001171: 
022385,001172:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022386,001173: 
022387,001174:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022388,001175: 
022389,001176: 24,3206  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022390,001177: 24,3206                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022391,001178: 24,3206           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022392,001179: 24,3207           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022393,001180: 24,3210           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022394,001181: 24,3211           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022395,001182: 24,3212           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022396,001183: 24,3213           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022397,001184: 24,3214           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022398,001185: 24,3215           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022399,001186: 24,3216           05353        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022400,001187: 24,3217           04022                           OCT      04022

022458,001245:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
022459,001246:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION

022468,001255:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE.

022667,001454:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                                                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022668,001455: 
022669,001456:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022670,001457: 
022671,001458:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022672,001459:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022673,001460:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022674,001461:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022675,001462:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022676,001463: 
022677,001464:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022678,001465:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022679,001466:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022680,001467:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022681,001468: 
022682,001469:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022683,001470:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022684,001471:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022685,001472:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022686,001473:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022687,001474: 
022688,001475:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022689,001476: 
022690,001477:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022691,001478:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022692,001479: 
022693,001480:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022694,001481: 
022695,001482:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022696,001483:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022697,001484:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022698,001485: 
022699,001486:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022700,001487: 
022701,001488:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022702,001489: 
022703,001490:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022704,001491: 
022705,001492:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022706,001493:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022707,001494: 
022708,001495:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND                                         
022709,001496:    4524           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
022710,001497:    4525           50000                           INDEX    0                                     
022711,001498:    4526           30001                           DCA      0

022713,001500:    4530           52062                           DXCH     ITEMP1

022715,001502: 
022716,001503:    4532           34740                           CAF      ANTENBIT                              #  SEE WHICH MODE RR IS IN.
022717,001504:    4533           70110                           MASK     RADMODES

022751,001538:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                         . IF EITHER:
022752,001539: 
022753,001540:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022754,001541:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022755,001542:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022756,001543:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022757,001544:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022758,001545:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022759,001546:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022760,001547:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022761,001548:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022762,001549:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022763,001550:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022764,001551:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022765,001552:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022766,001553:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022767,001554:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022768,001555:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022769,001556:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022770,001557:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022771,001558:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022772,001559:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022773,001560: 
022774,001561:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022775,001562: 
022776,001563:                                                                                                  #        L       TC      SETTRKF
022777,001564: 
022778,001565:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:  IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022779,001566: 
022780,001567:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
022781,001568: 
022782,001569:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022783,001570: 
022784,001571:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP
022785,001572: 
022786,001573:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)                                                          ED.

022823,001610:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022824,001611: 
022825,001612:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022826,001613: 
022827,001614:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022828,001615:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022829,001616:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022830,001617:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022831,001618:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022832,001619:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022833,001620:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022834,001621:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022835,001622:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022836,001623:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022837,001624:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022838,001625:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022839,001626: 
022840,001627:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022841,001628:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022842,001629:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022843,001630: 
022844,001631:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022845,001632: 
022846,001633:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022847,001634: 
022848,001635:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022849,001636: 
022850,001637:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022851,001638:                                                                                                  #        
022852,001639:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022853,001640: 
022854,001641:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022855,001642: 
022856,001643:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022857,001644: 
022858,001645: 24,3255                                           BANK     24                                    
022859,001646: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022860,001647: 25,2000                                           BANK

022872,001659:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022873,001660: 
022874,001661:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022875,001662:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022876,001663:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022877,001664:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022878,001665:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022879,001666:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022880,001667:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022881,001668:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022882,001669:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022883,001670:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022884,001671:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022885,001672:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022886,001673:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022887,001674:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022888,001675:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022889,001676:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022890,001677: 
022891,001678:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022892,001679: 
022893,001680:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022894,001681: 
022895,001682:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022896,001683: 
022897,001684:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022898,001685: 
022899,001686:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022900,001687: 
022901,001688:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022902,001689: 
022903,001690:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022904,001691: 
022905,001692:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022906,001693:

022910,001697: 25,2074           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.

022948,001735:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022949,001736: 
022950,001737:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022951,001738: 
022952,001739:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022953,001740:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022954,001741:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022955,001742:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022956,001743:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022957,001744:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022958,001745:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022959,001746:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022960,001747:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022961,001748:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022962,001749:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022963,001750:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022964,001751:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022965,001752:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022966,001753:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022967,001754:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022968,001755:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022969,001756:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022970,001757:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022971,001758:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022972,001759:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022973,001760:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022974,001761: 
022975,001762:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022976,001763: 
022977,001764:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022978,001765:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022979,001766: 
022980,001767:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022981,001768: 
022982,001769:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022983,001770: 
022984,001771:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022985,001772: 
022986,001773:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022987,001774: 
022988,001775:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022989,001776: 
022990,001777:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022991,001778: 
022992,001779:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
022993,001780: 
022994,001781:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022995,001782: 
022996,001783: 25,2127           02156        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
022997,001784: 
022998,001785:                                                                                                  #  ALARM 501 DELETED IN DANCE 279 PER PCR 97.
022999,001786:

023041,001828:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                         IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023042,001829: 
023043,001830:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023044,001831:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
023045,001832:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023046,001833:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023047,001834:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023048,001835:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023049,001836:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023050,001837:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023051,001838:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023052,001839:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023053,001840:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023054,001841:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023055,001842:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
023056,001843:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023057,001844:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023058,001845:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
023059,001846:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023060,001847:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023061,001848:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
023062,001849:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023063,001850: 
023064,001851:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023065,001852: 
023066,001853:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023067,001854:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023068,001855:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023069,001856:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
023070,001857: 
023071,001858:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023072,001859: 
023073,001860:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
023074,001861:

023076,001863:

023078,001865:

023080,001867:

023138,001925:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023139,001926: 
023140,001927:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023141,001928: 
023142,001929:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023143,001930:                                                                                                  #        RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
023144,001931:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023145,001932:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
023146,001933:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
023147,001934:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023148,001935:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023149,001936:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
023150,001937:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023151,001938:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
023152,001939:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023153,001940:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023154,001941:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023155,001942:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
023156,001943: 
023157,001944:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023158,001945:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
023159,001946:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
023160,001947:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023161,001948:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023162,001949: 
023163,001950:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023164,001951: 
023165,001952:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023166,001953: 
023167,001954:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023168,001955:

023178,001965:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)

023231,002018:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023232,002019: 
023233,002020:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023234,002021: 
023235,002022:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023236,002023:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023237,002024:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023238,002025:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023239,002026:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023240,002027:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023241,002028:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023242,002029:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023243,002030:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023244,002031:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023245,002032:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023246,002033:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023247,002034:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.

023341,002128:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                        R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023342,002129: 
023343,002130:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023344,002131: 
023345,002132:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023346,002133:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023347,002134:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023348,002135:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023349,002136:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023350,002137:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023351,002138:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023352,002139:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023353,002140:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023354,002141:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023355,002142:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023356,002143:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023357,002144:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023358,002145:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023359,002146:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023360,002147:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023361,002148:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023362,002149:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023363,002150:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023364,002151:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023365,002152:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023366,002153:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023367,002154: 
023368,002155:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023369,002156: 
023370,002157:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023371,002158:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
023372,002159:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023373,002160:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023374,002161: 
023375,002162:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023376,002163: 
023377,002164:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023378,002165: 
023379,002166:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023380,002167: 
023381,002168:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023382,002169:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023383,002170: 
023384,002171:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023385,002172: 
023386,002173:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023387,002174: 
023388,002175:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023389,002176:

023391,002178:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE - RETURNS
023392,002179:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                         CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.

023431,002218:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023432,002219: 
023433,002220:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023434,002221:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023435,002222:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023436,002223:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023437,002224:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023438,002225:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023439,002226:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023440,002227:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023441,002228:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023442,002229:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023443,002230:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023444,002231:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023445,002232:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023446,002233:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023447,002234:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023448,002235:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023449,002236:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023450,002237:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023451,002238:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023452,002239:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023453,002240:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023454,002241: 
023455,002242:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023456,002243: 
023457,002244:                                                                                                  #        FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
023458,002245: 
023459,002246:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023460,002247: 
023461,002248:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
023462,002249: 
023463,002250:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023464,002251:

023468,002255: 
023469,002256:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES
023470,002257:

023472,002259:
