023604,002391:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023605,002392: 
023606,002393:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023607,002394: 
023608,002395:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023609,002396:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023610,002397:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023611,002398:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023612,002399:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023613,002400:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023614,002401:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023615,002402:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023616,002403:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023617,002404:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023618,002405:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023619,002406:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023620,002407:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023621,002408:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023622,002409:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023623,002410:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023624,002411:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023625,002412:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023626,002413:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023627,002414:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023628,002415:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023629,002416:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023630,002417:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023631,002418:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023632,002419:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023633,002420: 
023634,002421:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023635,002422: 
023636,002423:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023637,002424:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023638,002425:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023639,002426: 
023640,002427:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023641,002428:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023642,002429: 
023643,002430:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023644,002431:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
023645,002432: 
023646,002433:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023647,002434: 
023648,002435:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023649,002436:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023650,002437: 
023651,002438:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023652,002439:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023653,002440:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023654,002441: 
023655,002442: 25,2573           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023701,002488:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023702,002489: 
023703,002490:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023704,002491: 
023705,002492:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023706,002493:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023707,002494:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023708,002495:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023709,002496:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023710,002497:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023711,002498:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023712,002499:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023713,002500:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023714,002501:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023715,002502:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023716,002503:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023717,002504:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023718,002505:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023719,002506:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023720,002507:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023721,002508:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023722,002509:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023723,002510:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023724,002511:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023725,002512:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023726,002513:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023727,002514:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023728,002515:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023729,002516:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023730,002517:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023731,002518:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023732,002519:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023733,002520:                                                                                                  #        CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023734,002521:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023735,002522:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023736,002523:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023737,002524:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023738,002525:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023739,002526:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023740,002527:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023741,002528:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023742,002529:

023819,002606:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS POINT WE HAVE A ROTATION VECTOR IN DISH AXES LYING IN THE TS PLANE.  CONVERT THIS TO A

023827,002614: 25,2722           74740                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A

024370,003157:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
024371,003158:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO. 2    BY J.D. COYNE   SDC     DATE 12-7-66
024372,003159: 
024373,003160:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024374,003161:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.
024375,003162:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
024376,003163:                                                                                                  #        3)      COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
024377,003164: 
024378,003165:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE      CALL
024379,003166:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1
024380,003167: 
024381,003168:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024382,003169:                                                                                                  #        LEMPREC, CSMPREC
024383,003170: 
024384,003171:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT_  RETURN TO CALLER + 2
024385,003172: 
024386,003173:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS_  NONE
024387,003174: 
024388,003175:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024389,003176: 
024390,003177:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT_
024391,003178:                                                                                                  #        LOS VECTOR (HALF UNIT) IN SM COORDINATES STORED IN RRTARGET
024392,003179:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR (METERS SCALED B-29) STORED IN MSLOV
024393,003180:                                                                                                  #        RRNBSW CLEARED
024394,003181: 
024395,003182:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZED ERASEABLE
024396,003183:                                                                                                  #        TDEC1 MUST CONTAIN THE TIME FOR EXTRAPOLATION
024397,003184:                                                                                                  #        SEE ORBITAL INTEGRATION ROUTINE
024398,003185: 
024399,003186:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS_
024400,003187:                                                                                                  #        MPAC DESTROYED BY THIS ROUTINE
024401,003188: 
024402,003189: 23,2314                                           BANK     23                                    
024403,003190: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
024404,003191: 24,2000                                           BANK

Page 565 

024406,003193: 24,3255                                           COUNT*   $$/LPS20                              
024407,003194: 
024408,003195: 24,3255           43020        LPS20.1            STQ      BOFF                                  
024409,003196: 24,3256           01757                                    LS21X                                 
024410,003197: 24,3257           01343                                    LOSCMFLG                              #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS NOT CALLED BY R21

024499,003286:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024500,003287:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024501,003288: 
024502,003289:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024503,003290:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024504,003291:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024505,003292:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024506,003293:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024507,003294: 
024508,003295:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024509,003296: 
024510,003297:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024511,003298:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
024512,003299:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024513,003300:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024514,003301:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024515,003302: 
024516,003303:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024517,003304: 
024518,003305:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024519,003306:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024520,003307:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024521,003308: 
024522,003309:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024523,003310:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024524,003311: 
024525,003312:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024526,003313:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024527,003314: 
024528,003315:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024529,003316:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024530,003317:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024531,003318:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024532,003319:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,AOG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS
024533,003320:                                                                                                  #                MKTIME - THE TIME OF THE RR READING, DP, IN CENTISECONDS
024534,003321: 
024535,003322:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024536,003323:                                                                                                  #        RNRAD, THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 569 

024538,003325:                                                                                                  #                1) RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
024539,003326:                                                                                                  #                2) RR RANGE RATE, SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024540,003327:                                                                                                  #        THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX, CDUY, CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
024541,003328:

024721,003508:

Page 574 

024723,003510:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024724,003511:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION - P20-25
024725,003512:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024726,003513: 
024727,003514:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024728,003515:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024729,003516:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024730,003517:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024731,003518: 
024732,003519:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024733,003520:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024734,003521:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024735,003522:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024736,003523:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024737,003524:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024738,003525:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024739,003526: 
024740,003527:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024741,003528:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024742,003529:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024743,003530: 
024744,003531:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024745,003532:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024746,003533:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024747,003534:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024748,003535:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024749,003536:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024750,003537: 
024751,003538:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024752,003539:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024753,003540:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024754,003541:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024755,003542:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024756,003543:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024757,003544:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024758,003545:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024759,003546:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024760,003547:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024761,003548:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN AOG
024762,003549:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024763,003550:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024764,003551:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024765,003552:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024766,003553: 
024767,003554:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024768,003555:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024769,003556:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

Page 575 

024771,003558:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T
024772,003559:

025164,003951: 
025165,003952:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025166,003953:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025167,003954:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025168,003955:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025169,003956: 
025170,003957:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025171,003958:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
025172,003959:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
025173,003960:

025176,003963:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR

Page 583 

025178,003965:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025179,003966:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025180,003967:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
025181,003968: 
025182,003969:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED

025296,004083: 
025297,004084:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES THE RELATIVE POSITION VECTOR BETWEEN THE CSM
025298,004085:                                                                                                  #  AND THE LM, LEAVING THE UNIT VECTOR IN THE PUSHLIST AND MPAC AND THE

025323,004110: 
025324,004111:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
025325,004112: 
025326,004113:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY

025388,004175:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025389,004176:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO 0                      BY P VOLANTE   SDC              DATE 1-15-67
025390,004177: 
025391,004178:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025392,004179: 
025393,004180:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025394,004181:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025395,004182:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025396,004183:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025397,004184: 
025398,004185:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025399,004186:

025401,004188: 
025402,004189:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM

025404,004191:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
025405,004192:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
025406,004193:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
025407,004194: 
025408,004195:                                                                                                  #  EXIT - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025409,004196:

025411,004198:

025413,004200:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED

025641,004428:

Page 594 

025643,004430:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025644,004431:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025645,004432: 
025646,004433:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025647,004434: 
025648,004435:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025649,004436:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025650,004437:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025651,004438:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025652,004439:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025653,004440:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025654,004441: 
025655,004442:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025656,004443: 
025657,004444:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025658,004445: 
025659,004446:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025660,004447:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025661,004448:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025662,004449:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025663,004450:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025664,004451:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025665,004452: 
025666,004453:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.

025873,004660:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025874,004661: 
025875,004662:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025876,004663:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025877,004664:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025878,004665:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025879,004666:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025880,004667: 
025881,004668:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025882,004669:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025883,004670: 
025884,004671: 32,2547                                           BANK     32                                    
025885,004672: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025886,004673: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025887,004674: 
025888,004675: 32,2547                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025889,004676: 32,2547  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025890,004677: 
025891,004678: 32,2547           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025892,004679: 32,2550           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025893,004680: 32,2551           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025894,004681: 
025895,004682: 32,2552           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025896,004683: 32,2553           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025897,004684: 32,2554           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025898,004685: 32,2555           12563                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025899,004686: 
025900,004687: 32,2556           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025901,004688: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025902,004689: 32,2560           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025903,004690: 32,2561           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025904,004691: 32,2562           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025905,004692: 
025906,004693: 32,2563           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025907,004694: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q

025909,004696: 32,2566           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025910,004697: 32,2567           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025911,004698: 32,2570           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025912,004699: 32,2571           12577                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025913,004700: 
025914,004701: 32,2572           00006                           EXTEND

025916,004703: 32,2574           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025917,004704: 32,2575           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025918,004705: 32,2576           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025919,004706: 
025920,004707: 32,2577           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025921,004708: 32,2600           12552                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025922,004709:

Page 601 

025924,004711:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025925,004712:

025927,004714: 32,2602           52155                           DXCH     MPAC

025933,004720:

025953,004740:

025957,004744:

Page 602 

025959,004746:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTE COSINE OF THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE PRESENT LOS AND THE RR BORESIGHT VECTOR, AND SET THE SELFTRACK ENABLE IF
025960,004747:                                                                                                  #  THE COSINE IS APPROXIMATELY COS(.5 DEG) OR GREATER (I.E. SMALLER ANGLE).
